 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Dec. 18, 2024 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>General Mills Reports Fiscal 2025 Second-quarter Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>and Updates Full-year Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> increased 1&nbsp;percent </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

increased 7&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

12&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Company updates full-year fiscal 2025 outlook to reflect increased investment to fund improved volume and
market share trends </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&sup1;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Please see Note 7 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release. </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS (Dec. 18, 2024) &#150;
General Mills, Inc. (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for its fiscal 2025 second quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We made important progress accelerating
our volume growth and market share trends in the first half of the year, including returning our North America Pet business to growth,&#148; said General Mills Chairman and Chief Executive Officer Jeff Harmening. &#147;To achieve and build on these
enterprise-wide gains, we&#146;ve made incremental investments to bring consumers greater value. While these investments lower our profit outlook for fiscal 2025, they better position General Mills for sustainable growth in fiscal 2026 and beyond.
Amidst a dynamic external environment, I&#146;m not only confident in our plans, but especially our teams, who are operating with agility and doing what&#146;s right for our consumers.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Guided by its purpose to make food the world loves, General Mills is executing its Accelerate strategy to drive sustainable, profitable growth
and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and win: boldly building brands, relentlessly innovating, unleashing scale, and
standing for good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is committed to reshaping its portfolio with strategic acquisitions and divestitures to
further enhance its growth profile. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Second Quarter Results Summary </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Results in the quarter were impacted by certain <B>favorable timing items</B> that are expected to reverse in the
second half of fiscal 2025. These include an increase in retailer inventory in North America Retail due in part to the Thanksgiving holiday shifting from the final week of the second quarter of fiscal 2024 to the first week of the third quarter of
fiscal 2025, as well as favorable trade and other expense timing. These items represented approximately a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.5-point</FONT> benefit to net sales and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">6-point</FONT> benefit to
operating profit in the quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 2&nbsp;percent to $5.2&nbsp;billion, driven by higher pound volume partially offset by
unfavorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were up 1&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was up 250 basis points to 36.9&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven primarily by Holistic
Margin Management (HMM) cost savings and favorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, partially offset by input cost inflation. Adjusted gross margin was up 130 basis points to
36.3&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven primarily by HMM cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation and unfavorable net price realization and mix. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $1.1&nbsp;billion was up 33&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by higher gross profit
dollars and a goodwill impairment charge a year ago, partially offset by higher selling, general, and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses. <B>Operating profit margin</B> of 20.6&nbsp;percent was up 480 basis points. Adjusted operating profit of
$1.1&nbsp;billion increased 7&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher adjusted SG&amp;A expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin was up 100 basis points to 20.3&nbsp;percent.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> of $796&nbsp;million were up 34&nbsp;percent and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was up 39&nbsp;percent to $1.42, driven primarily by higher operating profit and lower net shares outstanding, partially offset by a higher effective tax rate. Adjusted diluted EPS of $1.40 was up 12&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven
primarily by higher adjusted operating profit, lower net shares outstanding, and a lower adjusted effective tax rate. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Six Month
Results Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> of $10.1&nbsp;billion essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
results, with higher pound volume offset by unfavorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were also essentially in line with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> and adjusted gross margin were each up 70 basis points to 35.9&nbsp;percent of net sales,
driven primarily by HMM cost savings, partially offset by input cost inflation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $1.9&nbsp;billion was up 10&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by a goodwill impairment
charge a year ago and higher gross profit dollars this year, partially offset by higher SG&amp;A expenses. <B>Operating profit margin</B> of 18.9&nbsp;percent was up 160 basis points. Adjusted operating profit of $1.9&nbsp;billion increased
2&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by higher adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by higher adjusted SG&amp;A expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin was up 30 basis points to 19.1&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

EPS</B> was up 13&nbsp;percent to $2.45, driven primarily by higher operating profit and lower net shares outstanding, partially offset by a higher effective tax rate. Adjusted diluted EPS of $2.47 was up 6&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven
primarily by higher adjusted operating profit and lower net shares outstanding. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Operating Segment Results </U></B></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter net sales for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment of $3.3&nbsp;billion essentially matched
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results, with favorable net price realization and mix offset by lower pound volume. Organic net sales were up 1&nbsp;percent. Net sales outpaced Nielsen-measured retail sales by approximately 2 points
in the quarter, reflecting an increase in retailer inventory due in part to the impact of the later Thanksgiving holiday in fiscal 2025, as well as stronger growth in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-measured</FONT> channels. Net sales were up <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-single</FONT> digits for the U.S. Morning Foods operating unit and up <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-single</FONT> digits for U.S. Snacks. Net sales were down <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-single</FONT>
digits for U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions and were down <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-single</FONT> digits for Canada in constant currency. Segment operating profit of $862&nbsp;million essentially matched <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by HMM cost savings and favorable net price realization and mix, offset by input cost inflation, higher other supply chain costs, and lower
volume. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through six months, North America Retail segment net sales were down 1&nbsp;percent to
$6.3&nbsp;billion. Organic net sales essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels. Segment operating profit of $1.6&nbsp;billion was down 3&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by input
cost inflation, higher other supply chain costs, and lower volume, partially offset by HMM cost savings and favorable net price realization and mix. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Pet Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter net sales for
the North America Pet segment were up 5&nbsp;percent to $596&nbsp;million, driven by higher pound volume, partially offset by unfavorable net price realization and mix. Organic net sales were also up 5&nbsp;percent. Net sales performance outpaced <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all-channel</FONT> retail sales results by roughly 4 points, reflecting a rebuild of retailer inventory after significant prior-year reductions. Net sales in the quarter were up high-single digits for dry pet food, up <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-single</FONT> digits for wet pet food, and up <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-single</FONT> digits for pet treats. Segment operating profit of $139&nbsp;million was up 36&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by HMM cost
savings, higher volume, and lower other supply chain costs, partially offset by unfavorable net price realization and mix and higher SG&amp;A expenses including increased media investment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through six months, North America Pet segment net sales were up 2&nbsp;percent to $1.2&nbsp;billion. Organic net sales were also up
2&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit was up 21&nbsp;percent to $259&nbsp;million, driven primarily by HMM cost savings, lower other supply chain costs, and higher volume, partially offset by unfavorable net price realization and mix, higher
SG&amp;A expenses including increased media investment, and input cost inflation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Foodservice Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter net sales for the North America Foodservice segment were up 8&nbsp;percent to $630&nbsp;million. Organic net sales were also up 8&nbsp;percent,
with growth on breads, cereal, and frozen meals. Segment operating profit increased 24&nbsp;percent to $118&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through six months, North America Foodservice net sales increased 4&nbsp;percent to $1.2&nbsp;billion. Organic net sales were also up
4&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit was up 23&nbsp;percent to $190&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>International Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter net sales for the
International segment increased 1&nbsp;percent to $691&nbsp;million, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4-point</FONT> benefit from the Edgard&nbsp;&amp; Cooper acquisition. Organic net sales were down 3&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by
declines in China and Brazil, partially offset by growth in distributor markets and Europe&nbsp;&amp; Australia. Segment operating profit totaled $24&nbsp;million versus $35&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by unfavorable net price
realization and mix and higher SG&amp;A expenses, partially offset by HMM cost savings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through six months, International net sales
increased 1&nbsp;percent to $1.4&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> benefit from the Edgard&nbsp;&amp; Cooper acquisition. Organic net sales were down 2&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit totaled
$45&nbsp;million versus $85&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by unfavorable net price realization and mix and input cost inflation, partially offset by HMM cost savings and higher volume. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter
constant-currency net sales increased 2&nbsp;percent for Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW) and were up 1&nbsp;percent for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ). Combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT>
earnings from joint ventures were up 24&nbsp;percent to $30&nbsp;million, driven primarily by lower input costs and favorable net price realization and mix at CPW, partially offset by higher SG&amp;A expenses and lower volume at CPW and higher input
costs at HDJ. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other Income Statement Items </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Second-quarter unallocated corporate items totaled $65&nbsp;million net expense in fiscal 2025 compared to $157&nbsp;million net expense a year ago. Excluding <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled $80&nbsp;million net expense this year compared to
$103&nbsp;million net expense a year ago. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs totaled $1&nbsp;million in the second
quarter compared to $124&nbsp;million a year ago <I>(please see Note 3 below for more information on these charges)</I>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net interest
expense totaled $125&nbsp;million in the second quarter compared to $118&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by higher average long-term debt levels. The effective tax rate in the quarter was 20.1&nbsp;percent compared to 19.0&nbsp;percent
last year <I>(please see Note 6 below for more information on our effective tax rate)</I>. The second-quarter adjusted effective tax rate was 20.1&nbsp;percent compared to 20.8&nbsp;percent a year ago, driven primarily by favorable earnings mix by
jurisdiction in the second quarter of fiscal 2025. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation and Cash Returns </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash provided by operating activities totaled $1.8&nbsp;billion through six months of fiscal 2025 and was up 19&nbsp;percent from a year ago, driven primarily
by a change in accounts payable, partially offset by changes in inventory and other current assets. Capital investments totaled $301&nbsp;million compared to $294&nbsp;million a year ago. Dividends paid of $676&nbsp;million were down 2&nbsp;percent,
reflecting lower average shares outstanding. General Mills repurchased approximately 9&nbsp;million shares of common stock through six months of fiscal 2025 for a total of $600&nbsp;million compared to $1.3&nbsp;billion in share repurchases a year
ago. Average diluted shares outstanding in the first half decreased 4&nbsp;percent to 562&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2025 Outlook </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Amid an uncertain macroeconomic backdrop for consumers across its core markets, General Mills is focused on delivering remarkable experiences across its
leading food brands, resulting in sustainable improvement in volume growth and market share trends over time. Through the first six months of fiscal 2025, General Mills generated 1&nbsp;percent growth in organic pound volume, which represented a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4-point</FONT> improvement versus its fiscal 2024 performance. Additionally, it grew or maintained dollar market share in 38&nbsp;percent of its priority businesses in the second quarter, which represented a significant
improvement from fiscal 2024 levels. To support these improvements, the company has added targeted promotional investment &#150; above its original plans &#150; in certain priority categories to deliver greater value for consumers, while continuing
to invest in brand building above fiscal 2024 levels. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Based on the above assumptions, the company updated its full-year fiscal 2025 financial
targets&sup2;: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Organic net sales</B> are still expected to range between flat and up 1&nbsp;percent, with the company now
targeting the lower end of the range due to increased promotional investment. Organic net sales results in the second half are expected to include a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from the reversal of timing-related
benefits in the second quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GENERAL MILLS, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The accompanying Consolidated Financial Statements of General Mills, Inc. (we, us, our, General Mills, or the
Company) have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States for annual and interim financial information. In the opinion of management, all adjustments considered necessary for a fair presentation
have been included and are of a normal recurring nature. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the second quarter of fiscal 2025, we entered into a definitive agreement to acquire NX Pet Holding,
Inc., representing Whitebridge Pet Brands&#146; North America premium cat feeding and pet treating business for approximately $1&nbsp;billion (Whitebridge Pet Brands acquisition). We expect to close the transaction in the third quarter of fiscal
2025, subject to regulatory approval and other customary closing conditions. We intend to fund the acquisition with cash on hand. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter of fiscal 2025, we entered into definitive agreements to sell our North American yogurt businesses to affiliates of
Group Lactalis S.A. (Lactalis) and Sodiaal International (Sodiaal) for approximately $2&nbsp;billion. We expect to close these divestitures in calendar year 2025, subject to regulatory approvals and other customary closing conditions. We have
classified all assets and liabilities associated with our North American yogurt business as held for sale in our Consolidated Balance Sheets as of November&nbsp;24, 2024. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the fourth quarter of fiscal 2024, we acquired a pet food business in Europe for a purchase price of $434&nbsp;million, net of cash
acquired. During the first quarter of fiscal 2025, we paid $8&nbsp;million related to a purchase price holdback after certain closing conditions were met. We financed the transaction with cash on hand. We consolidated the business into our
Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $318&nbsp;million, an indefinite-lived brand intangible asset of $118&nbsp;million, and a finite-lived customer relationship asset of $14&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the
International segment and is not deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. We have conducted a preliminary assessment of the fair value of the acquired assets and liabilities of the business and we are
continuing our review of these items during the measurement period. If new information is obtained about facts and circumstances that existed at the acquisition date, the acquisition accounting will be revised to reflect the resulting adjustments to
current estimates of those items. The consolidated results are reported in our International operating segment on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-month</FONT> lag beginning in fiscal 2025. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

undertake any new restructuring actions. We recorded $1&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the second quarter of fiscal 2025 and $4&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended
November&nbsp;24, 2024, related to restructuring actions previously announced. We recorded $15&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the second quarter of fiscal 2024 and $25&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;26, 2023, related to previously announced restructuring actions. We expect these actions to be completed by the end of fiscal 2026. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In the second quarter of fiscal 2024, we recorded a $117&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> goodwill impairment
charge related to our Latin America reporting unit. </P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(4)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Unallocated corporate expenses totaled $65&nbsp;million in the second quarter of fiscal 2025, compared to
$157&nbsp;million in the same period in fiscal 2024. In the second quarter of fiscal 2025, we recorded a $29&nbsp;million net decrease in expense related to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories, compared to a $25&nbsp;million net increase in expense in the same period last year. We
recorded $3&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation adjustments on certain corporate investments in the second quarter of fiscal 2025, compared to $20&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation adjustments of certain corporate
investments in the second quarter of fiscal 2024. In addition, we recorded $9&nbsp;million of transaction costs related to the definitive agreement for the Whitebridge Pet Brands acquisition and definitive agreements to sell our North American
yogurt businesses in the second quarter of fiscal 2025, compared to $1&nbsp;million of transaction costs in the same period last year. We recorded $8&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in the second quarter of fiscal 2024. In addition, we
recorded $2&nbsp;million of integration costs related to the acquisition of a pet food business in Europe in the second quarter of fiscal 2025. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate expenses totaled $189&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended
November&nbsp;24, 2024, compared to $244&nbsp;million in the same period in fiscal 2024. In the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;24, 2024, we recorded a $1&nbsp;million net decrease in expense related to
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories, compared to a $20&nbsp;million net decrease in expense in the same period last year.
We recorded $4&nbsp;million of net losses related to valuation adjustments on certain corporate investments in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;24, 2024, compared to $22&nbsp;million of net losses
related to valuation adjustments and the loss on sale of certain corporate investments in the same period in fiscal 2024. In addition, we recorded $1&nbsp;million of restructuring charges and an immaterial amount of restructuring initiative
project-related costs in cost of sales in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;24, 2024, compared to $17&nbsp;million of restructuring charges and $1&nbsp;million of restructuring initiative
project-related costs in cost of sales in the same period last year. Compensation expense related to stock-based payments decreased in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;24, 2024, compared to the same
period in fiscal 2024. In the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;24, 2024, we recorded $9&nbsp;million of transaction costs related to the definitive agreement for the Whitebridge Pet Brands acquisition and
definitive agreements to sell our North American yogurt businesses, compared to $1&nbsp;million of transaction costs in the same period last year. We recorded $4&nbsp;million of integration costs related to the acquisition of a pet food business in
Europe in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> period ended November&nbsp;24, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our consolidated net sales and segment net
sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes. We believe that organic net sales
growth rates provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions, divestitures, and a
53rd&nbsp;fiscal week, when applicable, have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales growth rates, the relevant GAAP
measures, are included in our Operating Segment Results above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are presented excluding the impact of
foreign currency exchange (constant-currency). To present this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at the average exchange rates in
effect during the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year results in local currencies
multiplied by the change in the average foreign currency exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide useful information to investors
because they provide transparency to underlying performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT>
comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2025 outlook for organic net sales growth, adjusted
operating profit growth, adjusted diluted EPS growth, and free cash flow conversion are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including
the effect of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd week, when applicable. We are not able to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their
most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure without unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the actual impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates and the timing of
acquisitions and divestitures throughout fiscal 2025. The unavailable information could have a significant impact on our fiscal 2025 GAAP financial results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For fiscal 2025, we currently expect: foreign currency exchange rates (based on a blend of forward and forecasted rates and hedge positions)
and acquisitions and divestitures will have no material impact to net sales growth and restructuring charges to be immaterial. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting Comparability </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in
management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fiscal
2025 transaction costs related to the definitive agreement for the Whitebridge Pet Brands acquisition and definitive agreements to sell our North American yogurt businesses. Immaterial transaction costs incurred in fiscal 2024. Please see Note 2.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring charges and project-related costs </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges and project-related costs related to previously announced restructuring actions recorded in fiscal 2025 and fiscal 2024.
Please see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Acquisition integration costs </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Integration costs resulting from the acquisition of a pet food business in Europe recorded in fiscal 2025. Integration costs primarily
resulting from the acquisition of TNT Crust recorded in fiscal 2024. Please see Note 2. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Investment activity, net </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Valuation adjustments of certain corporate investments in fiscal 2025 and fiscal 2024. Please see Note 4. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions
recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Goodwill impairment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-cash</FONT> goodwill impairment charge related to our Latin America reporting unit in fiscal 2024. Please
see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Costs related to the fiscal 2023 voluntary recall of certain international <I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT></I> ice
cream products recorded in fiscal 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>CPW restructuring charges </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CPW restructuring charges related to previously announced restructuring actions. </P>
</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Operating Profit Growth and Related Constant-currency Growth Rate</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the measurement of our performance for incentive
compensation purposes. We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors because it is the operating profit measure we use to evaluate operating profit performance on a comparable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. The measure is evaluated on a constant-currency basis by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given the volatility in foreign currency exchange rates.&#8195; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our adjusted
operating profit growth on a constant-currency basis is calculated as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Net Sales Growth Rates for our Canada Operating Unit on a Constant-currency Basis</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe that this measure of our Canada operating unit net sales provides useful information to investors because it provides transparency to underlying
performance of our Canada operating unit within our North America Retail segment by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net sales growth rates for our Canada operating unit on a constant-currency basis are calculated as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="84%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt" ALIGN="center">

<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" COLSPAN="2" ALIGN="center" STYLE="border-bottom:1.00pt solid #000000"><B>Percentage&nbsp;Change&nbsp;in</B><br><B>Net Sales</B><br><B>as Reported</B></TD>

// Edgar(tm) Renderer was created by staff of the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.  Data and content created by government employees within the scope of their employment are not subject to domestic copyright protection. 17 U.S.C. 105.
var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
